1067| // ========== HORLOGE EN TEMPS RรEL ==========
1068| function updateClock() {
1069|     const now = new Date();
1070|     const options = {
1071|         weekday: 'long',
1072|         year: 'numeric',
1073|         month: 'long',
1074|         day: 'numeric',
1075|         hour: '2-digit',
1076|         minute: '2-digit',
1077|         second: '2-digit',
1078|         hour12: false
1079|     };
1080|     const formatted = now.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR', options);
1081|     const clockSpan = document.getElementById('currentDateTime');
1082|     if (clockSpan) clockSpan.textContent = formatted;
1083| }
1084| 
1085| // Mettre ร  jour l'horloge toutes les secondes
1086| setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
1087| updateClock(); // Appel immรฉdiat

1089| // Gestion des onglets
1090| function initTabs() {
1091|     const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');
1092|     tabs.forEach(btn => {
1093|         btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
1094|             tabs.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
1095|             btn.classList.add('active');
1096| 
1097|             document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => {
1098|                 content.classList.remove('active');
1099|             });
1100| 
1101|             const tabId = `tab-${btn.dataset.tab}`;
1102|             document.getElementById(tabId).classList.add('active');
1103| 
1104|             if (btn.dataset.tab === 'reports') loadReports();
1105|             if (btn.dataset.tab === 'logs') loadModerationLogs();
1106|         });
1107|     });
1108| }

1110| // ========== 7. UTILITAIRES ==========
1111| function escapeHtml(str) {
1112|     if (!str) return '';
1113|     return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function (m) {
1114|         if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
1115|         if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
1116|         if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
1117|         return m;
1118|     });
1119| }

6| function getCountryName(code) {

8|         'FR': 'Franรงais',

26| function displayMessage(text, type, fromPseudo = null, targetName = null) {
27|     const messageArea = document.getElementById('messageArea');
28|     if (!messageArea) return;
29| 
30|     messageArea.innerHTML = '';
31|     const div = document.createElement('div');
32|     div.className = 'current-message';
33| 
34|     if (type === 'received') {
35|         div.innerHTML = `<strong>โ๏ธ ${escapeHtml(fromPseudo)} :</strong> ${escapeHtml(text)}`;
36|         div.style.background = '#fff0e0';
37|         div.style.padding = '15px';
38|         div.style.borderRadius = '12px';
39|         currentReceivedMessage = text;
40|         currentReceivedFrom = fromPseudo;
41|     } else if (type === 'sent') {
42|         div.innerHTML = `<strong>๐ค Vous โ ${escapeHtml(targetName)} :</strong> ${escapeHtml(text)}`;
43|         div.style.background = '#e0f0ff';
44|         div.style.padding = '15px';
45|         div.style.borderRadius = '12px';
46|         currentReceivedMessage = null;
47|         currentReceivedFrom = null;
48|     }
49| 
50|     messageArea.appendChild(div);
51| }

132|         } else {

134|                 title: '๐ซ Bloquer',
135|                 message: `Bloquer ${pseudo} ? Vous ne recevrez plus ses messages.`,
136|                 onConfirm: () => {
137|                     // ๐ฅ APPEL ร LA FONCTION DE CHAT.JS
138|                     if (typeof window.blockUser === 'function') {
139|                         window.blockUser(pseudo);
140|                     } else {
141|                         console.error('โ window.blockUser non dรฉfinie');
142|                     }
143|                 }
144|             });
145|         }
146|     };
147| 
148|     // LIGNE 1 : Pseudo + icรดnes
149|     if (contactNameSpan) {
150|         contactNameSpan.innerHTML = '';
151|         const pseudoText = document.createTextNode(pseudo || '?');
152|         contactNameSpan.appendChild(pseudoText);
153|         const iconContainer = document.createElement('span');
154|         iconContainer.className = 'user-action-container';
155|         iconContainer.appendChild(reportIcon);
156|         iconContainer.appendChild(blockIcon);
157|         contactNameSpan.appendChild(iconContainer);
158|     }
159| 
160|     // LIGNE 2 : Toutes les autres infos (รขge, origine, genre, orientation, localitรฉ)
161|     if (contactAgeSpan) {
162|         const origineValue = (origine && origine !== 'undefined' && origine !== '' && origine !== 'null') ? getCountryName(origine) : 'NC';
163| 
164|         let genderText = '?';
165|         if (gender === 'G') genderText = 'Gay';
166|         else if (gender === 'H') genderText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Hรฉtรฉro' : 'Hetero');
167|         else if (gender === 'T') genderText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Transgenre' : 'Transgender');
168| 
169|         const orientationText = getOrientationText(orientation) || '?';
170|         const locationText = (location && location !== 'undefined' && location !== 'null') ? location : '';
171|         console.log('๐ DEBUG - location =', location, 'locationPrecise =', locationPrecise);
172|         const belgiumIcon = '<img src="/images/bel-img.png" style="width:18px; height:18px; display:inline-block; vertical-align:middle; margin-right:0px;">';
173| 
174|         // --- AFFICHAGE DE LA LOCALITร (corrigรฉ pour GPS) ---
175|         let displayLocation = '';
176| 
177|         // Si location = "GPS" ou contient "gรฉolocaliser", on utilise locationPrecise comme ville
178|         if (location === 'GPS' || (location && location.includes('gรฉolocaliser'))) {
179|             // locationPrecise = la commune prรฉcise (ex: Borchtlombeek)
180|             // location = la ville (ex: Roosdaal) ou "GPS"
181|             const city = locationPrecise || locationText || 'Localitรฉ';
182|             const commune = (locationPrecise && locationPrecise !== 'null' && locationPrecise !== 'undefined') ? locationPrecise : '';
183| 
184|             if (commune && commune !== city) {
185|                 displayLocation = `${commune} - ${city}`;
186|             } else {
187|                 displayLocation = city;
188|             }
189|         } else {
190|             // Cas normal (rรฉgion sรฉlectionnรฉe dans la liste)
191|             displayLocation = locationText || '';
192|             if (locationPrecise && locationPrecise !== 'null' && locationPrecise !== 'undefined') {
193|                 displayLocation = `${locationPrecise} - ${locationText}`;
194|             }
195|         }
196| 
197|         let infoLine = `${age || '?'} ans | ${origineValue} | ${genderText} | ${orientationText}`;
198| 
199|         if (displayLocation) {
200|             infoLine += ` | ${belgiumIcon} ${displayLocation}`;
201|         }
202| 
203|         contactAgeSpan.innerHTML = `( <i class="fas fa-birthday-cake"></i> ${infoLine} )`;
204|         contactAgeSpan.style.display = 'block';
205|         contactAgeSpan.style.marginTop = '5px';
206|     }
207| 
208|     // Cacher les anciens spans
209|     if (contactGenderSpan) {
210|         contactGenderSpan.style.display = 'none';
211|         contactGenderSpan.remove();
212|     }
213|     if (contactOrientationSpan) {
214|         contactOrientationSpan.style.display = 'none';
215|         contactOrientationSpan.remove();
216|     }

218|     // Purpose
219|     let purposeText = '';
220|     if (purpose === 'meeting') purposeText = '๐ฌ Rencontre';
221|     else if (purpose === 'flirt') purposeText = '๐ Flirt';

65| // Charger la liste des bloquรฉs depuis la base
66| async function loadBlockedUsers() {
67|     console.log('๐ loadBlockedUsers appelรฉe, user.pseudo =', user?.pseudo);  // โ LOG
68|     try {
69|         const response = await fetch('/api/blocked-list', {
70|             method: 'POST',
71|             headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
72|             body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo: user.pseudo })
73|         });
74|         const data = await response.json();
75|         console.log('๐ฅ Rรฉponse de /api/blocked-list:', data);  // โ LOG
76|         if (data.success) {
77|             window.blockedUsers = data.blocked || [];
78|             console.log('๐ Bloques chargรฉs depuis la base:', window.blockedUsers);
79|             updateBlockedList();
80|             socket.emit('get users list');
81|         }
82|     } catch (err) {
83|         console.error('โ Erreur chargement bloquรฉs:', err);
84|         window.blockedUsers = [];
85|     }

88| // Bloquer un utilisateur
89| window.blockUser = async function (pseudo) {
90|     console.log('๐ฅ blockUser appelรฉe pour', pseudo);
91| 
92|     if (pseudo === user.pseudo) {
93|         alert('Vous ne pouvez pas vous bloquer vous-mรชme.');
94|         return;
95|     }
96| 
97|     if (window.blockedUsers.includes(pseudo)) {
98|         alert(`${pseudo} est dรฉjร  bloquรฉ.`);
99|         return;
100|     }
101| 
102|     try {
103|         console.log('๐ค Appel ร  /api/block avec:', { blocker: user.pseudo, blocked: pseudo });
104|         const response = await fetch('/api/block', {
105|             method: 'POST',
106|             headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
107|             body: JSON.stringify({ blocker: user.pseudo, blocked: pseudo })
108|         });
109|         const data = await response.json();
110|         console.log('๐ฅ Rรฉponse de /api/block:', data);
111| 
112|         if (data.success) {
113|             window.blockedUsers.push(pseudo);
114|             updateBlockedList();
115|             if (currentTargetName === pseudo) {
116|                 messageInput.disabled = true;
117|                 sendBtn.disabled = true;
118|                 messageInput.placeholder = `๐ ${pseudo} est bloquรฉ. Dรฉbloquez-le dans les rรฉglages.`;
119|             }
120|             socket.emit('get users list');
121|             console.log(`๐ ${pseudo} bloquรฉ`);
122|         } else {
123|             // ๐ฅ NOUVEAU : Mรชme si l'API retourne une erreur "Dรฉjร  bloquรฉ", on met ร  jour l'interface
124|             if (data.error === 'Dรฉjร  bloquรฉ') {
125|                 if (!window.blockedUsers.includes(pseudo)) {
126|                     window.blockedUsers.push(pseudo);
127|                     updateBlockedList();
128|                     if (currentTargetName === pseudo) {
129|                         messageInput.disabled = true;
130|                         sendBtn.disabled = true;
131|                         messageInput.placeholder = `๐ ${pseudo} est bloquรฉ. Dรฉbloquez-le dans les rรฉglages.`;
132|                     }
133|                     socket.emit('get users list');
134|                     console.log(`๐ ${pseudo} dรฉjร  bloquรฉ (interface synchronisรฉe)`);
135|                 }
136|             } else {
137|                 alert(data.error || 'Erreur lors du blocage');
138|             }
139|         }
140|     } catch (err) {
141|         console.error('โ Erreur blocage:', err);
142|         alert('Erreur lors du blocage');
143|     }
144| };

146| // Dรฉbloquer un utilisateur
147| window.unblockUser = async function (pseudo) {
148|     console.log('๐ฅ unblockUser appelรฉe pour', pseudo);
149|     try {
150|         const response = await fetch('/api/unblock', {
151|             method: 'POST',
152|             headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
153|             body: JSON.stringify({ blocker: user.pseudo, blocked: pseudo })
154|         });
155|         const data = await response.json();
156|         if (data.success) {
157|             const index = window.blockedUsers.indexOf(pseudo);
158|             if (index > -1) {
159|                 window.blockedUsers.splice(index, 1);
160|             }
161|             updateBlockedList();
162|             // Si c'รฉtait le contact actuel, rรฉactiver l'envoi
163|             if (currentTargetName === pseudo) {
164|                 messageInput.disabled = false;
165|                 sendBtn.disabled = false;
166|                 messageInput.placeholder = `Message pour ${pseudo}...`;
167|             }
168|             // Rafraรฎchir la liste des utilisateurs
169|             socket.emit('get users list');
170|             console.log(`๐ ${pseudo} dรฉbloquรฉ`);
171|         } else {
172|             alert(data.error || 'Erreur lors du dรฉblocage');
173|         }
174|     } catch (err) {
175|         console.error('Erreur dรฉblocage:', err);
176|         alert('Erreur lors du dรฉblocage');
177|     }
178| };

201|     function setupButtons(onConfirm, onCancel) {
202|         const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('mg-modal-confirm');
203|         const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('mg-modal-cancel');
204|         const container = document.getElementById('mg-modal-container');
205| 
206|         if (confirmBtn) {
207|             const newConfirm = confirmBtn.cloneNode(true);
208|             confirmBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newConfirm, confirmBtn);
209|             newConfirm.onclick = () => {
210|                 container.style.display = 'none';
211|                 if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
212|             };
213|         }
214| 
215|         if (cancelBtn) {
216|             const newCancel = cancelBtn.cloneNode(true);
217|             cancelBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newCancel, cancelBtn);
218|             newCancel.onclick = () => {
219|                 container.style.display = 'none';
220|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
221|             };
222|         }
223| 
224|         container.onclick = (e) => {
225|             if (e.target === container) {
226|                 container.style.display = 'none';
227|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
228|             }
229|         };
230|     }

337|     // Charger l'historique des messages pour une conversation
338|     async function loadHistory(withPseudo) {
339|         try {
340|             const response = await fetch(`/api/messages/${encodeURIComponent(user.pseudo)}/${encodeURIComponent(withPseudo)}`);
341|             const messages = await response.json();
342| 
343|             // Nettoyer l'historique existant pour ce contact
344|             if (!conversationHistory[withPseudo]) {
345|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo] = [];
346|             } else {
347|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo] = [];
348|             }
349| 
350|             // Ajouter les messages chargรฉs
351|             messages.forEach(msg => {
352|                 const type = msg.from_pseudo === user.pseudo ? 'sent' : 'received';
353|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo].push({
354|                     text: msg.message,
355|                     type: type,
356|                     from: msg.from_pseudo,
357|                     to: msg.to_pseudo,
358|                     timestamp: new Date(msg.created_at)
359|                 });
360|             });
361| 
362|             updateHistoryDisplay();
363|         } catch (err) {
364|             console.error('Erreur chargement historique:', err);
365|         }
366| 
367|     }

415|     function updateUserBadge(warnsCount = 0) {
416|         const userBadge = document.getElementById('userBadge');
417|         if (!userBadge) return;
418| 
419|         // ๐ฅ Rรฉcupรฉrer la localitรฉ affichable
420|         let city = '?';
421|         if (user.location_name && user.location_name !== 'GPS' && user.location_name !== 'Me gรฉolocaliser pour plus de prรฉcision') {
422|             city = user.location_name;
423|         } else if (user.location_precise && user.location_precise !== 'null' && user.location_precise !== 'undefined') {
424|             // Si on a une commune prรฉcise, on l'utilise
425|             city = user.location_precise;
426|         } else {
427|             city = user.location_code || '?';
428|         }
429| 
430|         // Si on a une commune prรฉcise ET une ville diffรฉrente, on les combine
431|         if (user.location_precise && user.location_precise !== 'null' &&

877|     function showPrivatePopup(pseudo) {
878|         if (document.getElementById('privatePopup')) return;
879| 
880|         const chatPanel = document.querySelector('.chat-panel');
881|         if (!chatPanel) return;
882|

884|             chatPanel.style.position = 'relative';
885|         }

888|         if (!inputArea) return;
889| 
890|         const inputRect = inputArea.getBoundingClientRect();
891|         const chatRect = chatPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
892|         const topPosition = inputRect.bottom - chatRect.top;
893| 
894|         const popup = document.createElement('div');
895|         popup.id = 'privatePopup';
896|         popup.style.cssText = `
897|             position: absolute;
898|             top: ${topPosition + 5}px;
899|             left: 0;
900|             right: 0;
901|             background: #2c3e50;
902|             color: white;
903|             border-radius: 8px;
904|             padding: 10px 12px;
905|             z-index: 1000;
906|             font-family: 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;
907|             font-size: 12px;
908|             display: flex;
909|             justify-content: space-between;
910|             align-items: center;
911|             flex-wrap: wrap;
912|             gap: 8px;
913|             box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);
914|             opacity: 0;
915|             transform: translateY(-10px);
916|             transition: opacity 0.2s ease, transform 0.2s ease;
917|         `;

920|             <span>๐ฌ <strong>${pseudo}</strong> : 3 messages รฉchangรฉs. Passer en privรฉ ?</span>

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/utils.js

3| function escapeHtml(str) {
4|     if (!str) return '';
5|     return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function (m) {
6|         if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
7|         if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
8|         if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
9|         return m;
10|     });
11| }
12| 
13| function formatTime(date) {
14|     return date.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
15| }
16| 
17| function getOrientationSymbol(tendencies) {
18|     if (tendencies === 'A') return 'โฒ';
19|     if (tendencies === 'P') return 'โผ';
20|     return 'โฒโผ';
21| }
22| 
23| function getOrientationText(tendencies) {
24|     if (tendencies === 'A') return 'โฒ Actif';
25|     if (tendencies === 'P') return 'โผ Passif';
26|     return 'โฒโผ Versatile';
27| }

266|                 return str

268|                     .replace(/4/g, 'a').replace(/5/g, 's').replace(/7/g, 't')
269|                     .replace(/8/g, 'b').replace(/@/g, 'a').replace(/\$/g, 's');

272|             function isPseudoForbidden(pseudo, forbiddenWords) {
273|                 const lowerPseudo = pseudo.toLowerCase();
274| 
275|                 for (const forbidden of forbiddenWords) {
276|                     const lowerForbidden = forbidden.toLowerCase();
277| 
278|                     // Vรฉrification EXACTE : le pseudo doit รชtre le mot interdit
279|                     // OU le mot interdit est un mot sรฉparรฉ (avec des espaces ou tirets)
280|                     if (lowerPseudo === lowerForbidden) {
281|                         return true;
282|                     }
283| 
284|                     // Vรฉrifier si le mot interdit est un mot isolรฉ dans le pseudo
285|                     // (entourรฉ d'espaces, de tirets, ou en dรฉbut/fin)
286|                     const regex = new RegExp(`\\b${escapeRegex(lowerForbidden)}\\b`);
287|                     if (regex.test(lowerPseudo)) {
288|                         return true;
289|                     }
290|                 }
291|                 return false;
292|             }
293| 
294|             // Fonction utilitaire pour รฉchapper les caractรจres spรฉciaux dans une regex
295|             function escapeRegex(str) {
296|                 return str.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
297|             }

428|                             <small>${user.age} ans โข ${user.locationName || user.locationCode || '?'}</small>

442|     // ========== GรOLOCALISATION ==========
443|     document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
444| 
445|         // Rรฉfรฉrences des รฉlรฉments
446|         const locationSelect = document.getElementById('location');
447|         const gpsZone = document.getElementById('gpsZone');
448|         const gpsStatus = document.getElementById('gpsStatus');
449|         const gpsResult = document.getElementById('gpsResult');
450|         const detectedCity = document.getElementById('detectedCity');
451|         const displayPreview = document.getElementById('displayPreview');
452|         const gpsConsent = document.getElementById('gpsConsent');
453|         const gpsConfirm = document.getElementById('gpsConfirm');
454|         const gpsCancel = document.getElementById('gpsCancel');
455| 
456|         let detectedLat = null;
457|         let detectedLng = null;
458|         let detectedCityName = '';
459|         let detectedRegionName = '';  // โ la commune (county)
460| 
461|         // 1. Dรฉtecter le changement dans la liste dรฉroulante
462|         locationSelect.addEventListener('change', function () {
463|             if (this.value === 'GPS') {
464|                 // Afficher la zone GPS
465|                 gpsZone.style.display = 'block';

474|             } else {

478|                 gpsConfirm.disabled = true;
479|             }

482|         // 2. Fonction de gรฉolocalisation
483|         function startGeolocation() {
484|             if (!navigator.geolocation) {
485|                 gpsStatus.innerHTML = 'โ Votre navigateur ne supporte pas la gรฉolocalisation. Utilisez la liste dรฉroulante.';
486|                 return;
487|             }
488| 
489|             navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
490|                 // Succรจs
491|                 function (position) {
492|                     detectedLat = position.coords.latitude;
493|                     detectedLng = position.coords.longitude;
494| 
495|                     gpsStatus.innerHTML = '๐ Position trouvรฉe ! Je cherche le nom de la ville...';
496| 
497|                     // Appel ร  Nominatim pour avoir le nom de la ville
498|                     getCityName(detectedLat, detectedLng);
499| 
500|                 },
501|                 // Erreur
502|                 function (error) {
503|                     let msg = 'โ Erreur de gรฉolocalisation : ';
504|                     switch (error.code) {
505|                         case error.PERMISSION_DENIED:
506|                             msg += 'Vous avez refusรฉ l\'accรจs ร  votre position. Utilisez la liste dรฉroulante.';
507|                             break;
508|                         case error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE:
509|                             msg += 'Position indisponible. Vรฉrifiez votre connexion.';
510|                             break;
511|                         case error.TIMEOUT:
512|                             msg += 'Temps รฉcoulรฉ. Rรฉessayez.';
513|                             break;
514|                         default:
515|                             msg += error.message;
516|                     }
517|                     gpsStatus.innerHTML = msg;
518|                 },
519|                 {
520|                     enableHighAccuracy: true,
521|                     timeout: 10000,
522|                     maximumAge: 0
523|                 }
524|             );
525|         }

527|         function getCityName(lat, lng) {
528|             const url = `/api/geocode?lat=${lat}&lng=${lng}`;
529| 
530|             fetch(url)
531|                 .then(response => response.json())
532|                 .then(data => {
533|                     console.log('๐ก Rรฉponse Google Maps:', data);
534| 
535|                     if (data.status === 'OK' && data.results.length > 0) {
536|                         // On prend le premier rรฉsultat (le plus prรฉcis)
537|                         // === NOUVEAU CODE ===
538|                         // ๐ฅ On prend le rรฉsultat le PLUS PRรCIS (viewport le plus petit)
539|                         const sortedResults = [...data.results].sort((a, b) => {
540|                             const sizeA = (a.geometry.viewport.northeast.lat - a.geometry.viewport.southwest.lat) *
541|                                 (a.geometry.viewport.northeast.lng - a.geometry.viewport.southwest.lng);
542|                             const sizeB = (b.geometry.viewport.northeast.lat - b.geometry.viewport.southwest.lat) *
543|                                 (b.geometry.viewport.northeast.lng - b.geometry.viewport.southwest.lng);
544|                             return sizeA - sizeB;
545|                         });
546|                         const result = sortedResults[0];
547|                         console.log('๐ Rรฉsultat le PLUS PRรCIS sรฉlectionnรฉ:', result.formatted_address);
548|                         const components = result.address_components;
549| 
550|                         // --- RรCUPรRATION DES COMPOSANTS ---
551|                         const trouver = (type) => components.find(c => c.types.includes(type))?.long_name;
552| 
553|                         const locality = trouver("locality"); // Roosdaal
554|                         const sublocality = trouver("sublocality") || trouver("sublocality_level_1"); // Pamel
555|                         const postalCode = trouver("postal_code"); // 1760
556|                         const country = trouver("country"); // Belgique
557| 
558|                         // ๐ฅ NOUVEAU : Rรฉcupรฉrer les localitรฉs du code postal
559|                         const postcodeLocalities = data.results.find(r => r.types.includes("postal_code"))?.postcode_localities || [];
560| 
561|                         console.log('๐ Locality:', locality);
562|                         console.log('๐ Sublocality:', sublocality);
563|                         console.log('๐ Postcode Localities:', postcodeLocalities);
564| 
565|                         // --- DรTERMINATION DE LA COMMUNE PRรCISE ---
566|                         let communePrecise = locality;
567| 
568|                         // Prioritรฉ 1: sublocality (Pamel, Borchtlombeek, Strijtem)
569|                         if (sublocality && sublocality !== locality) {
570|                             communePrecise = sublocality;
571|                         }
572|                         // Prioritรฉ 2: postcode_localities (si sublocality n'existe pas)
573|                         else if (postcodeLocalities.length > 0 && postcodeLocalities[0] !== locality) {
574|                             communePrecise = postcodeLocalities[0];
575|                         }
576| 
577|                         console.log('โ Commune prรฉcise trouvรฉe:', communePrecise);
578| 
579|                         // --- AFFICHAGE ---
580|                         gpsStatus.style.display = 'none';
581|                         gpsResult.style.display = 'block';
582|                         detectedCity.textContent = locality;
583|                         document.getElementById('detectedCounty').textContent = communePrecise;
584| 
585|                         // OPTION 1 : juste la ville
586|                         document.getElementById('choiceRegionLabel').textContent = locality;
587| 
588|                         // OPTION 2 : commune prรฉcise + ville (si diffรฉrente)
589|                         let option2 = locality;
590|                         if (communePrecise && communePrecise !== locality) {
591|                             option2 = `${communePrecise} - ${locality}`;
592|                         } else if (country) {
593|                             option2 = `${locality} - ${country}`;
594|                         }
595|                         document.getElementById('choicePreciseLabel').textContent = option2;
596| 
597|                         // Rรฉinitialiser les radios
598|                         document.querySelectorAll('input[name="locationChoice"]').forEach(el => el.checked = false);
599|                         document.getElementById('gpsConsent').checked = false;
600|                         document.getElementById('gpsConfirm').disabled = true;
601|                         gpsConsent.disabled = false;
602| 
603|                         // Stocker pour confirmation
604|                         detectedCityName = locality;
605|                         detectedRegionName = communePrecise;
606| 
607|                         // Message informatif
608|                         const infoMsg = document.createElement('div');
609|                         infoMsg.style.cssText = 'font-size: 0.8em; color: #666; margin-top: 5px;';
610|                         infoMsg.innerHTML = `
611|                     โน๏ธ <strong>Option 1:</strong> ${locality}<br>
612|                     โน๏ธ <strong>Option 2:</strong> ${option2}
613|                 `;
614|                         const oldMsg = document.querySelector('.gps-info-msg');
615|                         if (oldMsg) oldMsg.remove();
616|                         infoMsg.className = 'gps-info-msg';
617|                         document.querySelector('#gpsResult')?.appendChild(infoMsg);
618| 
619|                     } else {
620|                         gpsStatus.innerHTML = 'โ Erreur Google Maps';
621|                     }
622|                 })
623|                 .catch(error => {
624|                     gpsStatus.innerHTML = 'โ Erreur';
625|                     console.error(error);
626|                 });
627|         }

645|             if (!detectedCityName) {

647|                 return;
648|             }

654|             }

657|             let locationPreciseValue = null;
658|

661|                 locationNameValue = detectedCityName;      // ex: "Dilbeek"
662|                 locationPreciseValue = null;
663|             } else {
664|                 // Option 2 : commune + ville
665|                 if (detectedRegionName && detectedRegionName !== detectedCityName) {
666|                     locationNameValue = detectedCityName;          // ex: "Dilbeek"
667|                     locationPreciseValue = detectedRegionName;     // ex: "Bekkerzeel"
668|                 } else {
669|                     locationNameValue = detectedCityName;
670|                     locationPreciseValue = null;
671|                 }
672|             }
673|

675|             console.log('๐ Sauvegarde GPS - locationName:', locationNameValue);
676|             console.log('๐ Sauvegarde GPS - locationPrecise:', locationPreciseValue);
677|

680|             if (!hiddenInput) {
681|                 hiddenInput = document.createElement('input');
682|                 hiddenInput.type = 'hidden';
683|                 hiddenInput.id = 'location_precise_hidden';
684|                 hiddenInput.name = 'location_precise';
685|                 document.getElementById('loginForm').appendChild(hiddenInput);
686|             }
687|             hiddenInput.value = locationPreciseValue !== null ? locationPreciseValue : '';
688|

690|             // On crรฉe une option pour la ville si elle n'existe pas
691|             const locationSelect = document.getElementById('location');
692|             let optionExists = false;
693|             for (let opt of locationSelect.options) {
694|                 if (opt.value === locationNameValue) {
695|                     optionExists = true;
696|                     break;
697|                 }
698|             }
699|             if (!optionExists) {
700|                 const newOption = document.createElement('option');
701|                 newOption.value = locationNameValue;
702|                 newOption.textContent = locationNameValue;
703|                 locationSelect.appendChild(newOption);
704|             }
705|             locationSelect.value = locationNameValue;
706|             locationSelect.disabled = false; // Ne pas dรฉsactiver
707| 
708|             // Afficher le rรฉsumรฉ
709|             const displayText = locationPreciseValue ? `${locationPreciseValue} - ${locationNameValue}` : locationNameValue;
710| 
711|             gpsZone.innerHTML = `
712|         <div style="padding: 10px; background: #e8f5e9; border-radius: 5px; color: #2e7d32;">
713|             โ Localisation confirmรฉe : <strong>${locationNameValue}</strong>
714|             <br><small>Votre profil affichera : ${displayText}</small>
715|         </div>
716|     `;
717|         });

750|     // ===== RECHERCHE MANUELLE AVEC AUTOCOMPLETE =====
751|     document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
752|         const switchToManualBtn = document.getElementById('switchToManualBtn');
753|         const manualSearchZone = document.getElementById('manualSearchZone');
754|         const manualLocationInput = document.getElementById('manualLocationInput');
755|         const manualResults = document.getElementById('manualResults');
756|         const suggestionsContainer = document.getElementById('autocompleteSuggestions');
757| 
758|         let autocompleteService = null;
759|         let sessionToken = null;
760|         let isSuggestionSelected = false;
761| 
762|         // Initialiser le service d'autocomplete
763|         function initAutocompleteService() {
764|             if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.maps && google.maps.places) {
765|                 autocompleteService = new google.maps.places.AutocompleteService();
766|                 sessionToken = new google.maps.places.AutocompleteSessionToken();
767|                 console.log('โ Autocomplete service initialisรฉ');
768|             } else {
769|                 console.log('โณ En attente de Google Maps...');
770|                 setTimeout(initAutocompleteService, 500);
771|             }
772|         }
773| 
774|         function loadGooglePlaces() {
775|             if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.maps && google.maps.places) {
776|                 initAutocompleteService();
777|             } else {
778|                 console.log('โณ En attente de Google Maps...');
779|                 setTimeout(function () {
780|                     if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.maps && google.maps.places) {
781|                         initAutocompleteService();
782|                     }
783|                 }, 1000);
784|             }
785|         }
786| 
787|         // ๐ฅ RECHERCHE EN TEMPS RรEL (autocomplete) - BELGIQUE UNIQUEMENT
788|         if (manualLocationInput) {
789|             manualLocationInput.addEventListener('input', function () {
790|                 const query = this.value.trim();
791| 
792|                 if (query.length < 2) {
793|                     suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
794|                     return;
795|                 }
796| 
797|                 if (!autocompleteService) {
798|                     loadGooglePlaces();
799|                     return;
800|                 }
801| 
802|                 // ๐ง๐ช RESTRICTION ร LA BELGIQUE
803|                 const request = {
804|                     input: query,
805|                     types: ['(cities)'],
806|                     componentRestrictions: { country: 'be' },
807|                 };
808| 
809|                 autocompleteService.getPlacePredictions(request, function (predictions, status) {
810|                     if (status === google.maps.places.PlacesServiceStatus.OK && predictions && predictions.length > 0) {
811|                         // Filtrer pour รชtre sรปr d'avoir que des villes belges
812|                         const belgianResults = predictions.filter(pred =>
813|                             pred.terms.some(term =>
814|                                 term.value === 'Belgique' ||
815|                                 term.value === 'Belgium' ||
816|                                 term.value === 'Belgiรซ'
817|                             )
818|                         );
819| 
820|                         if (belgianResults.length > 0) {
821|                             displaySuggestions(belgianResults);
822|                         } else {
823|                             // Aucun rรฉsultat belge
824|                             suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'block';
825|                             suggestionsContainer.innerHTML = `
826|                         <div class="suggestion-item" style="color:#888;font-style:italic;cursor:default;text-align:center;padding:20px;">
827|                             ๐ง๐ช Aucune ville belge trouvรฉe pour "<strong>${query}</strong>"
828|                         </div>
829|                     `;
830|                         }
831|                     } else {
832|                         suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
833|                     }
834|                 });
835|             });
836| 
837|             // ===== Cacher les suggestions quand on perd le focus =====
838|             manualLocationInput.addEventListener('blur', function () {
839|                 setTimeout(() => {
840|                     if (!isSuggestionSelected) {
841|                         suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
842|                     }
843|                     isSuggestionSelected = false;
844|                 }, 300);
845|             });
846| 
847|             // ===== Afficher les suggestions quand on regagne le focus =====
848|             manualLocationInput.addEventListener('focus', function () {
849|                 if (this.value.trim().length >= 2) {
850|                     this.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
851|                 }
852|             });
853| 
854|             // ===== Gรฉrer la touche รchap pour fermer les suggestions =====
855|             manualLocationInput.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
856|                 if (e.key === 'Escape') {
857|                     suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
858|                     this.blur();
859|                 }
860|             });
861| 
862| 
863|         }
864| 
865|         // ๐ฅ Afficher les suggestions - VERSION AMรLIORรE
866|         function displaySuggestions(predictions) {
867|             if (!predictions || predictions.length === 0) {
868|                 suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
869|                 return;
870|             }
871| 
872|             console.log('๐ Affichage de', predictions.length, 'suggestions');
873| 
874|             let html = '';
875|             predictions.forEach((pred, index) => {
876|                 const description = pred.description;
877|                 const placeId = pred.place_id;
878|                 const isLast = index === predictions.length - 1;
879|                 html += `
880|             <div class="suggestion-item" data-place-id="${placeId}" data-description="${description}" 
881|                  style="${isLast ? 'border-bottom: none;' : ''}">
882|                 ${description}
883|             </div>
884|         `;
885|             });
886| 
887|             suggestionsContainer.innerHTML = html;
888|             suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'block';
889|             suggestionsContainer.scrollTop = 0;
890| 
891|             // ๐ฅ DEBUG - Log pour vรฉrifier que la fonction s'exรฉcute
892|             console.log('โ Suggestions affichรฉes, container display =', suggestionsContainer.style.display);
893|             console.log('๐ฆ Container HTML:', suggestionsContainer.innerHTML.substring(0, 100) + '...');
894| 
895|             // Ajouter les รฉvรฉnements de clic sur les suggestions
896|             document.querySelectorAll('.suggestion-item').forEach(item => {
897|                 item.addEventListener('mousedown', function (e) {
898|                     e.preventDefault();
899|                     e.stopPropagation();
900|                     isSuggestionSelected = true;
901| 
902|                     const description = this.dataset.description;
903|                     const placeId = this.dataset.placeId;
904| 
905|                     manualLocationInput.value = description;
906|                     suggestionsContainer.style.display = 'none';
907| 
908|                     // Lancer la recherche avec le lieu sรฉlectionnรฉ
909|                     rechercherLocaliteAvecPlaceId(placeId, description);
910|                 });
911| 
912|                 item.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
913|                     this.style.background = '#e8f5e9';
914|                 });
915| 
916|                 item.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
917|                     this.style.background = 'white';
918|                 });
919|             });
920|         }
921|

923| 
924|         // Liste des 19 communes de Bruxelles
925|         const communesBruxelles = [
926|             'Anderlecht', 'Auderghem', 'Berchem-Sainte-Agathe', 'Bruxelles',
927|             'Etterbeek', 'Evere', 'Forest', 'Ganshoren', 'Ixelles', 'Jette',
928|             'Koekelberg', 'Molenbeek-Saint-Jean', 'Saint-Gilles',
929|             'Saint-Josse-ten-Noode', 'Schaerbeek', 'Uccle',
930|             'Watermael-Boitsfort', 'Woluwe-Saint-Lambert', 'Woluwe-Saint-Pierre'
931|         ];
932| 
933|         function rechercherLocalite(query) {
934|             // Recherche uniquement par nom de ville
935|             const queryString = String(query).trim();
936| 
937|             // Vรฉrifier si l'utilisateur n'a tapรฉ qu'un code postal (4 chiffres)
938|             if (/^[0-9]{4}$/.test(queryString)) {
939|                 manualResults.innerHTML = `
940|         <div class="result-error">
941|             โ ๏ธ <strong>Code postal "${queryString}" dรฉtectรฉ</strong><br>
942|             Tapez รฉgalement le nom de la ville associรฉe.<br>
943|             <small>Exemple : "1020 Bruxelles" ou "Laeken 1020"</small>
944|         </div>
945|     `;
946|                 manualResults.style.display = 'block';
947|                 return;
948|             }
949| 
950|             const searchQuery = `${queryString}, Belgique`;
951|             console.log('๐ Recherche de la ville:', searchQuery);
952| 
953|             const url = `/api/geocode?address=${encodeURIComponent(searchQuery)}&language=fr`;
954| 
955|             manualResults.innerHTML = '<div class="result-loading">๐ Recherche en Belgique...</div>';
956|             manualResults.style.display = 'block';
957| 
958|             fetch(url)
959|                 .then(response => response.json())
960|                 .then(data => {
961|                     console.log('๐ก Rรฉsultat recherche manuelle:', data);
962| 
963|                     if (data.status === 'OK' && data.results && data.results.length > 0) {
964|                         const options = new Set();
965| 
966|                         data.results.forEach(result => {
967|                             // ๐ฅ RECHERCHE DES COMPOSANTS
968|                             const locality = result.address_components.find(c =>
969|                                 c.types.includes('locality') || c.types.includes('postal_town')
970|                             )?.long_name;
971| 
972|                             const sublocality = result.address_components.find(c =>
973|                                 c.types.includes('sublocality') || c.types.includes('sublocality_level_1')
974|                             )?.long_name;
975| 
976|                             // ๐ฅ NOUVEAU : neighborhood (quartier)
977|                             const neighborhood = result.address_components.find(c =>
978|                                 c.types.includes('neighborhood')
979|                             )?.long_name;
980| 
981|                             // Vรฉrifier si locality est une commune bruxelloise
982|                             const isLocalityBruxelles = communesBruxelles.some(
983|                                 commune => commune.toLowerCase() === locality?.toLowerCase()
984|                             );
985| 
986|                             // Vรฉrifier si sublocality est une commune bruxelloise
987|                             const isSublocalityBruxelles = communesBruxelles.some(
988|                                 commune => commune.toLowerCase() === sublocality?.toLowerCase()
989|                             );
990| 
991|                             // Vรฉrifier si neighborhood est une commune bruxelloise
992|                             const isNeighborhoodBruxelles = communesBruxelles.some(
993|                                 commune => commune.toLowerCase() === neighborhood?.toLowerCase()
994|                             );
995| 
996|                             // --- CAS 1 : locality existe ---
997|                             if (locality) {
998|                                 // Si locality est une commune bruxelloise
999|                                 if (isLocalityBruxelles) {
1000|                                     // ๐ฅ AJOUT : Si locality est "Bruxelles", on n'ajoute PAS "Bruxelles, Bruxelles"
1001|                                     if (locality !== 'Bruxelles') {
1002|                                         const option = `${locality}, Bruxelles`;
1003|                                         if (!options.has(option)) {
1004|                                             options.add(option);
1005|                                         }
1006|                                     }
1007|                                     // On ajoute "Bruxelles" seul
1008|                                     if (!options.has('Bruxelles')) {
1009|                                         options.add('Bruxelles');
1010|                                     }
1011|                                 } else {
1012|                                     // Ville normale โ on propose la ville seule
1013|                                     if (!options.has(locality)) {
1014|                                         options.add(locality);
1015|                                     }
1016|                                 }
1017|                             }
1018|

1020|                             if (sublocality && sublocality !== locality) {

1024|                                     if (!options.has(combo)) {

1028|                                         options.add('Bruxelles');
1029|                                     }

1033|                                     if (!options.has(combo)) {
1034|                                         options.add(combo);
1035|                                     }
1036|                                 }
1037|                             }

1053|                                     if (!options.has(combo)) {
1054|                                         options.add(combo);
1055|                                     }
1056|                                 }

1076|                                         โ Aucune localitรฉ trouvรฉe pour "${query}".<br>
1077|                                         <small>Vรฉrifiez l'orthographe ou essayez avec le code postal et la ville.</small>
1078|                                     </div>

1081|                 })

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/fingerprint-source.js

1| ๏ปฟimport FingerprintJS from '@fingerprintjs/fingerprintjs';
2| 
3| (async () => {
4|     try {
5|         const fp = await FingerprintJS.load();
6|         const result = await fp.get();
7|         const visitorId = result.visitorId;
8|         sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', visitorId);
9|         window.currentFingerprint = visitorId;
10|         console.log('๐ Fingerprint gรฉnรฉrรฉ:', visitorId);
11|     } catch (err) {
12|         console.error('โ Erreur fingerprint:', err);
13|         // Fallback temporaire (รฉvite de bloquer l'utilisateur)
14|         const fallback = 'temp_' + Date.now();
15|         sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fallback);
16|         window.currentFingerprint = fallback;
17|     }
18| })();

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/common.js

1| ๏ปฟ// ========== COMMON - MeetGay ==========
2| // Fonctions et dรฉtecteurs partagรฉs entre les pages (login, chat, etc.)
3| 
4| (function () {
5|     // ========== 1. Dรฉtection de la rรฉsolution d'รฉcran ==========
6|     function detectResolution() {
7|         const width = window.innerWidth;
8|         const height = window.innerHeight;
9|         const resolution = `${width}x${height}`;
10|         sessionStorage.setItem('screen_resolution', resolution);
11|         console.log(`๐ฑ Rรฉsolution dรฉtectรฉe : ${resolution}`);
12|         return resolution;
13|     }
14| 
15|     // ========== 2. รchapper le HTML (sรฉcuritรฉ) ==========
16|     function escapeHtml(str) {
17|         if (!str) return '';
18|         return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, (m) => {
19|             if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
20|             if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
21|             if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
22|             return m;
23|         });
24|     }
25| 
26|     // ========== 3. Formater l'heure (HH:MM) ==========
27|     function formatTime(date) {
28|         if (!date) return '';
29|         const d = new Date(date);
30|         return `${d.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${d.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
31|     }
32| 
33|     // ========== 4. Exรฉcuter la dรฉtection au chargement ==========
34|     if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
35|         document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', detectResolution);
36|     } else {
37|         detectResolution();
38|     }
39| 
40|     // ========== 5. Exposer les fonctions globalement ==========
41|     window.common = {
42|         escapeHtml: escapeHtml,
43|         formatTime: formatTime,
44|         detectResolution: detectResolution,
45|         getResolution: () => sessionStorage.getItem('screen_resolution')
46|     };
47| })();

25|     // Configurer les boutons une fois que le DOM est prรชt
26|     function setupButtons(onConfirm, onCancel) {
27|         const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('mg-popup-confirm');
28|         const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('mg-popup-cancel');
29|         const container = document.getElementById('mg-popup-container');
30| 
31|         if (confirmBtn) {
32|             const newConfirm = confirmBtn.cloneNode(true);
33|             confirmBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newConfirm, confirmBtn);
34|             newConfirm.onclick = () => {
35|                 container.style.display = 'none';
36|                 if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
37|             };
38|         }
39| 
40|         if (cancelBtn) {
41|             const newCancel = cancelBtn.cloneNode(true);
42|             cancelBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newCancel, cancelBtn);
43|             newCancel.onclick = () => {
44|                 container.style.display = 'none';
45|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
46|             };
47|         }
48| 
49|         // Clic sur le fond noir pour fermer (optionnel)
50|         container.onclick = (e) => {
51|             if (e.target === container) {
52|                 container.style.display = 'none';
53|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
54|             }
55|         };
56|     }
57| 
58|     // API publique
59|     window.MGModal = {

61|             createPopupStructure();
62|

65|             const messageEl = document.getElementById('mg-popup-message');
66|

69|             messageEl.textContent = options.message || 'Message par dรฉfaut';
70| 
71|             // Configurer les boutons
72|             setupButtons(options.onConfirm, options.onCancel);
73| 
74|             // Afficher
75|             container.style.display = 'flex';
76|         },
77| 
78|         hide: function () {
79|             const container = document.getElementById('mg-popup-container');

1| ๏ปฟ// ========== CHAT SCRIPT - MeetGay ==========
2| // Centralise toute la logique restante du chat (fingerprint, traductions, historique coulissant, menus)
3| 
4| (function () {
5|     // ========== 1. Fingerprint (si non dรฉjร  fait par fp-bundle.js) ==========
6|     (async function () {
7|         let fingerprint = sessionStorage.getItem('fingerprint');
8|         if (!fingerprint) {
9|             try {
10|                 // Si FingerprintJS est dรฉjร  chargรฉ globalement, on l'utilise
11|                 if (typeof FingerprintJS !== 'undefined') {
12|                     const fp = await FingerprintJS.load();
13|                     const result = await fp.get();
14|                     fingerprint = result.visitorId;
15|                 } else {
16|                     console.warn('FingerprintJS non trouvรฉ, utilisation d\'un identifiant alรฉatoire');
17|                     fingerprint = 'fp_' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2);
18|                 }
19|                 sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fingerprint);
20|                 window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
21|             } catch (err) {
22|                 console.error('โ Fingerprint impossible ร  gรฉnรฉrer:', err);
23|                 fingerprint = 'fallback_' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2);
24|                 sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fingerprint);
25|                 window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
26|             }
27|         } else {
28|             window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
29|         }
30|     })();
31| 
32|     // ========== 2. Vรฉrifier si l'utilisateur est en session ==========

54|             placeholderInput: "Klik eerst op een pseudoniem...",

78|

80|         if (messageInput) messageInput.placeholder = t.placeholderInput;

83|     // ========== 5. Gestion de l'historique coulissant ==========
84|     document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
85|         const historyInner = document.getElementById('historyInner');
86|         const historyTab = document.getElementById('historyTab');
87|         const closeBtn = document.getElementById('closeInnerSlider');
88| 
89|         // รtat du dรฉcalage du bouton (false = position normale)
90|         let tabOffset = false;
91| 
92|         // Fonction pour dรฉcaler ou remettre le bouton
93|         function toggleTabOffset() {
94|             if (!historyTab) return;
95|             if (tabOffset) {
96|                 historyTab.style.right = '0';
97|                 tabOffset = false;
98|             } else {
99|                 historyTab.style.right = '-10px';
100|                 tabOffset = true;
101|             }
102|         }
103| 
104|         if (historyInner) {
105|             historyInner.classList.remove('open');
106|         }
107| 
108|         if (historyTab && historyInner) {
109|             historyTab.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
110|                 e.stopPropagation();
111|                 historyInner.classList.toggle('open');
112|                 toggleTabOffset(); // โ dรฉcaler/remettre le bouton au clic
113|             });
114|         }
115| 
116|         if (closeBtn && historyInner) {
117|             closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
118|                 historyInner.classList.remove('open');
119|                 // Quand on ferme avec la croix, on remet aussi le bouton
120|                 if (historyTab) historyTab.style.right = '0';
121|                 tabOffset = false;
122|             });
123|         }
124|     });

126|     // ========== 6. Gรฉnรฉration des menus (fenรชtre droite) ==========
127|     // Note : ce bloc utilise import, il doit รชtre dans un script type="module"
128|     // On va donc le charger dynamiquement
129|     // ========== 6. Gรฉnรฉration des menus (fenรชtre droite) ==========
130|     (function initMenus() {
131|         const menuList = document.getElementById('newMenusList');
132|         const windowContent = document.getElementById('windowContent');
133|         const windowPlaceholder = document.getElementById('windowPlaceholder');
134| 
135|         if (!menuList) {
136|             console.warn('Menu list not found, retrying in 500ms');
137|             setTimeout(initMenus, 500);
138|             return;
139|         }
140| 
141|         // Charger les donnรฉes des menus via fetch (car import ne fonctionne pas ici)
142|         fetch('/js/menus-data.js')
143|             .then(response => response.text())
144|             .then(data => {
145|                 // Extraire les variables exportรฉes (approche simple)
146|                 const exports = {};
147|                 const moduleCode = data.replace(/export const /g, 'exports.');
148|                 new Function('exports', moduleCode)(exports);
149| 
150|                 const menus = exports.menus;
151|                 const contents = exports.contents;
152| 
153|                 if (!menus) return;
154| 
155|                 menus.forEach(menu => {
156|                     const item = document.createElement('div');
157|                     item.className = 'new-menu-item';
158|                     item.innerHTML = `<i class="fas ${menu.icon}"></i><span>${menu.title}</span>`;
159|                     item.onclick = () => {
160|                         windowPlaceholder.style.display = 'none';
161|                         windowContent.style.display = 'block';
162|                         windowContent.innerHTML = contents[menu.id] || '<div class="dynamic-content"><h3>Contenu ร  venir</h3></div>';
163|                     };
164|                     menuList.appendChild(item);
165|                 });
166|             })
167|             .catch(err => console.error('Erreur chargement menus-data.js:', err));
168|     })();

171|     (function () {
172|         'use strict';
173| 
174|         // Lecture des media queries CSS (vous les modifiez dans le CSS)
175|         const desktopMQ = window.matchMedia('(min-width: 1081px)');
176|         const mobileMQ = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 350px)');
177|         // Entre 351px et 1080px = mode desktop รฉgalement
178| 
179|         // === VERSION DESKTOP ===
180|         function initDesktopVersion() {
181|             const nav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
182|             const panel = document.getElementById('navSettingsPanel');
183|             const settingsBtn = document.getElementById('navSettingsBtn');
184|             const navButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav button:not(#toggleNavBtn)');
185| 
186|             let isPanelOpen = false;
187|             let animationTimer = null;
188| 
189|             if (nav) nav.style.display = 'flex';
190| 
191|             // Bouton bleu
192|             const oldToggleBtn = document.getElementById('toggleNavBtn');
193|             if (oldToggleBtn) {
194|                 const newToggleBtn = oldToggleBtn.cloneNode(true);
195|                 oldToggleBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newToggleBtn, oldToggleBtn);
196|                 newToggleBtn.onclick = function (e) {
197|                     e.preventDefault();
198|                     const isVisible = navButtons[0]?.classList.contains('hidden');
199|                     navButtons.forEach(btn => {
200|                         if (isVisible) btn.classList.remove('hidden');
201|                         else btn.classList.add('hidden');
202|                     });
203|                     localStorage.setItem('mobileNavVisible', !isVisible);
204|                 };
205|             }
206| 
207|             function setPanelOrientation() {
208|                 if (!panel || !nav) return;
209|                 const pos = nav.getAttribute('data-position') || 'bottom';
210|                 panel.classList.remove('horizontal', 'vertical');
211|                 if (pos === 'left' || pos === 'right') {
212|                     panel.classList.add('vertical');
213|                 } else {
214|                     panel.classList.add('horizontal');
215|                 }
216|             }
217| 
218|             function positionPanel() {
219|                 if (!panel || !nav) return;
220|                 const navRect = nav.getBoundingClientRect();
221|                 const panelW = panel.offsetWidth;
222|                 const panelH = panel.offsetHeight;
223|                 const pos = nav.getAttribute('data-position') || 'bottom';
224|                 if (panelW === 0 || panelH === 0) return;
225| 
226|                 let top, left;
227|                 switch (pos) {
228|                     case 'left':
229|                         left = navRect.right + 8;
230|                         top = navRect.top + (navRect.height / 2) - (panelH / 2);
231|                         break;
232|                     case 'right':
233|                         left = navRect.left - panelW - 8;
234|                         top = navRect.top + (navRect.height / 2) - (panelH / 2);
235|                         break;
236|                     case 'top':
237|                         left = navRect.left;
238|                         top = navRect.bottom + 8;
239|                         break;
240|                     default:
241|                         left = navRect.left;
242|                         top = navRect.top - panelH - 8;
243|                         break;
244|                 }
245| 
246|                 if (left < 5) left = 5;
247|                 if (left + panelW > window.innerWidth - 5) left = window.innerWidth - panelW - 5;
248|                 if (top < 5) top = 5;
249|                 if (top + panelH > window.innerHeight - 5) {
250|                     if (pos === 'top') top = navRect.top - panelH - 8;
251|                     else if (pos === 'bottom') top = navRect.bottom + 8;
252|                     else top = window.innerHeight - panelH - 5;
253|                 }
254| 
255|                 panel.style.top = top + 'px';
256|                 panel.style.left = left + 'px';
257|             }
258| 
259|             function openPanel() {
260|                 if (!panel) return;
261|                 panel.style.display = 'flex';
262|                 isPanelOpen = true;
263|                 setPanelOrientation();
264|                 positionPanel();
265|             }
266| 
267|             function closePanel() {
268|                 if (!panel) return;
269|                 panel.style.display = 'none';
270|                 isPanelOpen = false;
271|                 if (animationTimer) clearTimeout(animationTimer);
272|             }
273| 
274|             function togglePanel(e) {
275|                 e.stopPropagation();
276|                 if (isPanelOpen) closePanel();
277|                 else openPanel();
278|             }
279| 
280|             function setNavPosition(position) {
281|                 if (!nav) return;
282|                 nav.setAttribute('data-position', position);
283|                 localStorage.setItem('mobileNavPosition', position);
284|                 if (isPanelOpen) {
285|                     if (animationTimer) clearTimeout(animationTimer);
286|                     animationTimer = setTimeout(() => {
287|                         setPanelOrientation();
288|                         positionPanel();
289|                         animationTimer = null;
290|                     }, 320);
291|                 }
292|             }
293| 
294|             function loadSavedSettings() {
295|                 const savedPos = localStorage.getItem('mobileNavPosition');
296|                 if (savedPos && ['top', 'bottom', 'left', 'right'].includes(savedPos)) {
297|                     nav.setAttribute('data-position', savedPos);
298|                 } else {
299|                     nav.setAttribute('data-position', 'bottom');
300|                 }
301|                 const savedVis = localStorage.getItem('mobileNavVisible');
302|                 if (savedVis === 'true') navButtons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.add('hidden'));
303|                 else if (savedVis === 'false') navButtons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('hidden'));
304|             }
305| 
306|             function resetAll() {
307|                 closePanel();
308|                 localStorage.removeItem('mobileNavPosition');
309|                 localStorage.removeItem('mobileNavVisible');
310|                 location.reload();
311|             }
312| 
313|             function handleClickOutside(e) {
314|                 if (!isPanelOpen) return;
315|                 if (!nav.contains(e.target) && !panel.contains(e.target)) closePanel();
316|             }
317| 
318|             function scrollToTarget(e) {
319|                 const btn = e.currentTarget;
320|                 const targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');
321|                 if (!targetId) return;
322|                 e.preventDefault();
323|                 const target = document.getElementById(targetId);
324|                 if (target) {
325|                     closePanel();
326|                     const offset = nav.getAttribute('data-position') === 'top' ? nav.offsetHeight + 20 : 80;
327|                     const pos = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - offset;
328|                     window.scrollTo({ top: pos, behavior: 'smooth' });
329|                 }
330|             }
331| 
332|             if (nav && panel) {
333|                 loadSavedSettings();
334|                 if (settingsBtn) settingsBtn.onclick = togglePanel;
335|                 document.getElementById('navPosTop')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('top'));
336|                 document.getElementById('navPosBottom')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('bottom'));
337|                 document.getElementById('navPosLeft')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('left'));
338|                 document.getElementById('navPosRight')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('right'));
339|                 document.getElementById('navReset')?.addEventListener('click', resetAll);
340|                 document.querySelectorAll('[data-target]').forEach(btn => {
341|                     btn.addEventListener('click', scrollToTarget);
342|                 });
343|                 document.addEventListener('click', handleClickOutside);
344|                 window.addEventListener('resize', () => { if (isPanelOpen) positionPanel(); });
345|             }
346|         }
347| 
348|         // === VERSION MOBILE (trรจs petits รฉcrans) ===
349|         function initMobileVersion() {
350|             const oldNav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
351|             if (oldNav) oldNav.style.display = 'none';
352| 
353|             let menuBtn = document.getElementById('mobileMenuBtn');
354|             if (!menuBtn) {
355|                 menuBtn = document.createElement('button');
356|                 menuBtn.id = 'mobileMenuBtn';
357|                 menuBtn.innerHTML = 'โฐ';
358|                 document.body.appendChild(menuBtn);
359|             }
360| 
361|             let panel = document.getElementById('mobileNavPanel');
362|             if (!panel) {
363|                 panel = document.createElement('div');
364|                 panel.id = 'mobileNavPanel';
365|                 panel.innerHTML = `
366|                 <div class="mobile-panel-buttons">
367|                     <button data-target="connectes">๐ฅ<span>Connectรฉs</span></button>
368|                     <button data-target="chat">๐ฌ<span>Chat</span></button>
369|                     <button data-target="new-window">๐ฆ<span>Nouveau</span></button>
370|                     <button data-target="menus">๐<span>Menus</span></button>
371|                 </div>
372|             `;
373|                 document.body.appendChild(panel);
374|             }
375| 
376|             let isOpen = false;
377| 
378|             function openPanel() {
379|                 panel.classList.add('open');
380|                 isOpen = true;
381|             }
382| 
383|             function closePanel() {
384|                 panel.classList.remove('open');
385|                 isOpen = false;
386|             }
387| 
388|             function togglePanel() {
389|                 if (isOpen) closePanel();
390|                 else openPanel();
391|             }
392| 
393|             function scrollToTarget(e) {
394|                 const btn = e.currentTarget;
395|                 const targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');
396|                 if (!targetId) return;
397|                 e.preventDefault();
398|                 const target = document.getElementById(targetId);
399|                 if (target) {
400|                     const pos = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 70;
401|                     window.scrollTo({ top: pos, behavior: 'smooth' });
402|                 }
403|             }
404| 
405|             menuBtn.addEventListener('click', togglePanel);
406|             document.querySelectorAll('#mobileNavPanel [data-target]').forEach(btn => {
407|                 btn.addEventListener('click', scrollToTarget);
408|             });
409| 
410|             document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
411|                 if (isOpen && !panel.contains(e.target) && e.target !== menuBtn) {
412|                     closePanel();
413|                 }
414|             });
415|         }
416| 
417|         // === LANCEMENT (basรฉ sur les media queries CSS) ===
418|         function detectAndInit() {
419|             if (mobileMQ.matches) {
420|                 initMobileVersion();
421|             } else {
422|                 initDesktopVersion();
423|             }
424|         }
425| 
426|         detectAndInit();
427| 
428|         // === REDIMENSIONNEMENT ===
429|         let resizeTimer;
430|         desktopMQ.addEventListener('change', function () {
431|             if (resizeTimer) clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
432|             resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 150);
433|         });
434|         mobileMQ.addEventListener('change', function () {
435|             if (resizeTimer) clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
436|             resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 150);
437|         });
438|     })();
439| 
440| })();

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/admin-login.html

1| <!DOCTYPE html>
2| <html lang="fr">
3| 
4| <head>
5|     <meta charset="UTF-8">
6|     <title>Login Admin - MeetGay</title>
7|     <!-- CSS communs -->
8|     <link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/common/reset.css">
9| 
10|     <!-- CSS spรฉcifique admin-login -->
11|     <link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/pages/admin-login.css">
12| </head>
13| 
14| <body>
15|     <div class="login-box">
16|         <h1>๐ Admin Login</h1>
17|         <input type="text" id="adminUsername" placeholder="Nom d'utilisateur">
18|         <input type="password" id="adminPassword" placeholder="Mot de passe">
19|         <button onclick="loginAdmin()">Se connecter</button>
20|         <div id="errorMsg" class="error"></div>
21|     </div>
22| 
23|     <script>
24|         async function loginAdmin() {
25|             const username = document.getElementById('adminUsername').value;
26|             const password = document.getElementById('adminPassword').value;
27|             const errorDiv = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
28| 
29|             if (!username || !password) {
30|                 errorDiv.textContent = 'Veuillez entrer nom d\'utilisateur et mot de passe';
31|                 return;
32|             }
33| 
34|             try {
35|                 const response = await fetch('/api/admin/login', {
36|                     method: 'POST',
37|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
38|                     body: JSON.stringify({ username, password })
39|                 });
40| 
41|                 const data = await response.json();
42| 
43|                 if (data.success) {
44|                     // โ ๏ธ PLUS DE TOKEN, REDIRECTION SIMPLE
45|                     window.location.href = '/admin.html';
46|                 } else {
47|                     errorDiv.textContent = data.error || 'Identifiants incorrects';
48|                 }
49|             } catch (err) {
50|                 errorDiv.textContent = 'Erreur de connexion';
51|             }
52|         }
53|     </script>
54| </body>
55| 
56| </html>

130|                 resolutionGroup.style.display = 'block';
131|                 userEnvGroup.style.display = 'block';
132|             } else {
133|                 resolutionGroup.style.display = 'none';
134|                 userEnvGroup.style.display = 'none';
135|             }

139|         toggleTechFields(); // Initialisation au chargement
140| 
141|         // ========== Envoi du formulaire ==========
142|         contactForm.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
143|             e.preventDefault();
144| 
145|             const formData = {
146|                 name: document.getElementById('name').value.trim(),
147|                 email: document.getElementById('email').value.trim(),
148|                 subject: subjectSelect.value,
149|                 message: document.getElementById('message').value.trim(),
150|                 resolution: resolutionField.value,
151|                 userEnv: document.getElementById('userEnv').value.trim()
152|             };
153| 
154|             // Si le sujet est "bug", on ajoute les infos techniques dans le message
155|             if (formData.subject === 'bug') {
156|                 const resolution = sessionStorage.getItem('screen_resolution') || `${window.innerWidth}x${window.innerHeight}`;
157|                 const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
158|                 formData.message += `\n\n--- Informations techniques (automatique) ---\nRรฉsolution : ${resolution}\nNavigateur : ${userAgent}`;
159|             }
160| 
161|             // Validation
162|             if (!formData.name || !formData.email || !formData.subject || !formData.message) {
163|                 showStatus('โ Veuillez remplir tous les champs obligatoires', 'error');
164|                 return;
165|             }
166| 
167|             if (!formData.email.includes('@')) {
168|                 showStatus('โ Email invalide', 'error');
169|                 return;
170|             }
171| 
172|             const submitBtn = document.querySelector('.submit-btn');
173|             submitBtn.disabled = true;
174|             submitBtn.textContent = 'โณ Envoi en cours...';
175| 
176|             try {
177|                 const response = await fetch('/api/contact', {
178|                     method: 'POST',
179|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
180|                     body: JSON.stringify(formData)
181|                 });
182| 
183|                 const data = await response.json();
184| 
185|                 if (response.ok && data.success) {
186|                     showStatus('โ Message envoyรฉ ! Nous vous rรฉpondrons rapidement.', 'success');
187|                     contactForm.reset();
188|                     // Remettre les champs techniques en รฉtat aprรจs reset
189|                     toggleTechFields();
190|                 } else {
191|                     showStatus('โ Erreur : ' + (data.error || 'Rรฉessayez plus tard'), 'error');
192|                 }
193|             } catch (err) {
194|                 console.error('Erreur envoi:', err);
195|                 showStatus('โ Erreur rรฉseau. Vรฉrifiez votre connexion.', 'error');
196|             } finally {
197|                 submitBtn.disabled = false;
198|                 submitBtn.textContent = '๐จ Envoyer le message';
199|             }
200|         });
201|
